shared_focus = {
	id = BAT_the_hour_is_upon_us
	icon = GFX_goal_BAT_the_hour_is_upon_us
	x = 8
	y = 0
	cost = 4.40
	bypass = {
	    has_global_flag = equestrian_civil_war
	}
	
	ai_will_do = { 
	    factor = 10 
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BAT_the_hour_is_upon_us"
		swap_ideas = {
		    remove_idea = BAT_bitter_remnants
		    add_idea = BAT_the_hour_is_upon_us_idea
		}
		hidden_effect = {
		    country_event = {
			    id = bat.8
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
	    FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL 
		FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS
		FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT
	}
}

		    limit = {

			    id = bat.9

		}
	}
	search_filters = {

	icon = GFX_goal_BAT_limited_diplomacy
	x = -3
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BAT_emergency_session
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { 
	    focus = BAT_emergency_session 
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 14
		modifier = {
			has_global_flag = HIP_mountain_awakes_global_flag
			factor = 2
		}
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BAT_limited_diplomacy"
		country_event = {
			id = bat.56
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_idea = civilian_economy 
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = civilian_economy
		        add_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation 
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
		        add_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
			}
		}
		else = {
		    swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
		        add_idea = war_economy
			}
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
	    FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT
        FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY
        FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL		
	}
}

	icon = GFX_goal_BAT_COM_council
	x = -2
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = BAT_d24
	cost = 2.90
	prerequisite = { 
		focus = BAT_d24
	}
	available = { 
		if = {
		    limit = {
			    has_country_flag = BAT_the_troubles_flag
			}
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = BAT_6_paramilitary_group_neutralised_tp
				check_variable = {
                    var = BAT_paramilitaries_dealt_with
                    value = 6
                    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
			}
		}
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 8
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BAT_d25"
		if = {
		    limit = {
				has_idea = BAT_moral_army_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = BAT_moral_army_1
				add_idea = BAT_moral_army_2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		    limit = {
				has_idea = BAT_moral_army_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = BAT_moral_army_2
				add_idea = BAT_moral_army_3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
		    limit = {
				has_idea = BAT_moral_army_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = BAT_moral_army_3
				add_idea = BAT_moral_army_4
			}
		}
		else = {
		    add_ideas = BAT_moral_army_1
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
        FOCUS_FILTER_ARMY_BONUS
		FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY
		FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT
	}
}

shared_focus = {
	id = BAT_d28
	icon = GFX_goal_BAT_COM_bomber
	x = 2
	y = 1

	prerequisite = {

	}
	available = {

		    limit = {
			    has_country_flag = BAT_the_troubles_flag

				tooltip = BAT_6_paramilitary_group_neutralised_tp

                    value = 6

                }
			}
		}
		has_completed_focus = BAT_b27
	}
	
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 8
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus BAT_d28"
		swap_ideas = {
		    remove_idea = BAT_bomb_them_into_the_stone_age
			add_idea = BAT_bomb_them_into_the_stone_age_2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
			}
			set_technology = {
				early_bombs = 1
				engines_1 = 1
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = bomber_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = medium_air
			}
			generic_early_tac_bomber = yes
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_airframe_0
				variant_name = "Early Tactical Bomber"
				amount = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "By Blood Alone"
				NOT = {
					has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
				}
			}
			set_technology = {
				iw_medium_airframe = 1
				early_bombs = 1
				engines_1 = 1
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = bomber_bonus
				bonus = 3.0
				uses = 1
				category = medium_air
			}
			generic_early_tac_bomber = yes
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_airframe_0
				variant_name = "Early Tactical Bomber"
				amount = 40
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_tech = early_bomber
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = bomber_bonus
				bonus = 1.0
				uses = 2
				category = tactical_bomber
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_airframe
				amount = 40
				producer = BAT
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_technology = {
				early_bomber = 1
			}
			add_tech_bonus = {
				name = bomber_bonus
				bonus = 3.0
				uses = 1
				category = tactical_bomber
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = medium_plane_airframe

			}
